             <h2 class="text-over-image__headline">
              Powering Progress
             </h2>
             <p class="text-over-image__text">
              Shell’s strategy to accelerate the transition of our business to net-zero emissions, in step with society. Powering Progress is designed to create value for shareholders, customers and wider society.
             </p>

            <div class="component__body text-over-image__body">
             <h2 class="text-over-image__headline">
              Powering industry with help from the sun
             </h2>
             <p class="text-over-image__text">
              Shell’s first solar project in the Middle East is helping to power a smelting company in northern Oman and cutting its carbon emissions in the process.
             </p>
             <div class="colour--palette-0 text-over-image__button-wrapper">
              <a class="text-over-image__button atomic--button-link" href="/inside-energy/powering-omani-industry-with-help-from-the-sun.html">
               <span class="atomic--button-link-wrapper">
                <span class="atomic--button-link-label text-label">
                 Read more
                </span>
               </span>
              </a>
             </div>

            <div class="component__body text-over-image__body">
             <h2 class="text-over-image__headline">
              Road freight: a journey to lower emissions
             </h2>
             <p class="text-over-image__text">
              It accounts for about 9% of global carbon emissions, and road freight volume could double by 2050. So how can the sector decarbonise? We asked the world’s leading experts for their viewpoints.
             </p>
             <div class="colour--palette-0 text-over-image__button-wrapper">
              <a class="text-over-image__button atomic--button-link" href="/energy-and-innovation/the-energy-future/decarbonising-road-freight.html">
               <span class="atomic--button-link-wrapper">
                <span class="atomic--button-link-label text-label">
                 Read more
                </span>
               </span>
              </a>
             </div>

                  <img alt="" class="default-image" loading="lazy" src="/promos/poweringprogress/climate-target/_jcr_content/pagePromo/image.img.960.jpeg/1612984741056/our-climate-target.jpeg?imwidth=960"/>
                 </picture>
                </noscript>
               </div>
              </a>
             </div>
             <div class="promo-list__text">
              <h3>
               <a class="text-link" href="/energy-and-innovation/the-energy-future/our-climate-target.html">
                <span>
                 Our climate target
                </span>
               </a>
              </h3>
              <p>
               Shell’s target is to become a net-zero emissions energy business by 2050, in step with society.
              </p>
             </div>
            </div>

               <a class="text-link" href="/energy-and-innovation/natural-gas/liquefied-natural-gas-lng/lng-outlook-2021.html">
                <span>
                 Shell LNG Outlook 2021
                </span>
               </a>
              </h3>
              <p>
               Global demand for liquefied natural gas rose in 2020, despite the unprecedented volatility caused by the COVID-19 pandemic. Read more.
